import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback, useMemo } from "react";

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   STORAGE HOOK
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function useStorage(key, initial) {
  const [val, setVal] = useState(() => {
    try { const s = localStorage.getItem(key); return s ? JSON.parse(s) : initial; }
    catch { return initial; }
  });
  const set = useCallback((v) => {
    const next = typeof v === "function" ? v(val) : v;
    setVal(next);
    try { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(next)); } catch {}
  }, [key, val]);
  return [val, set];
}

const cache = {};
async function loadChunk(id) {
  if (!cache[id]) cache[id] = CHUNKS[id]?.() ?? [];
  return cache[id];
}
async function getModSorular(modId) {
  const map = {
    karma: ["c1","c2","c3","c4","c5","c6","c7","c8","c9","c10","c11","c12"],
    deneme: ["c1","c2","c3","c4","c5","c6","c7","c8","c9","c10","c11","c12"],
    c1:["c1"],c2:["c2"],c3:["c3"],c4:["c4"],c5:["c5"],c6:["c6"],c7:["c7"],c8:["c8"],c9:["c9"],c10:["c10"],c11:["c11"],c12:["c12"]
  };
  const ids = map[modId] || [];
  const all = (await Promise.all(ids.map(loadChunk))).flat();
  return [...all].sort(()=>Math.random()-.5);
}

function xpHesapla(kalan,maxSure,zorluk){ const b={kolay:8,orta:15,zor:25}[zorluk]??12; return b+(kalan>maxSure*.7?10:kalan>maxSure*.4?5:0); }
function xpToLevel(xp){ return Math.floor(xp/120)+1; }

const CSS=`
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Cinzel:wght@600;700&family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700&display=swap');
*,*::before,*::after{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0}

const STARS=Array.from({length:55},(_,i)=>({id:i,x:Math.random()*100,y:Math.random()*100,r:Math.random()*1.8+.4,op:Math.random()*.4+.08,dur:(Math.random()*3+2).toFixed(1)}));
function StarCanvas(){return(<div style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,pointerEvents:"none",zIndex:0,overflow:"hidden"}}>{STARS.map(s=><div key={s.id} style={{position:"absolute",left:`${s.x}%`,top:`${s.y}%`,width:s.r*2,height:s.r*2,borderRadius:"50%",background:"#C9A84C",opacity:s.op,animation:`pulse ${s.dur}s ease-in-out infinite`}}/>)}</div>);}

function XPBar({xp}){
  const lv=xpToLevel(xp),pct=((xp%120)/120)*100;
  return(<div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:10,minWidth:0,width:"100%"}}>
    <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#C9A84C,#E8C66A)",borderRadius:8,padding:"3px 10px",fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"#07070F",whiteSpace:"nowrap"}}>LV {lv}</div>
    <div style={{flex:1,height:5,background:"rgba(255,255,255,0.08)",borderRadius:3,overflow:"hidden"}}><div style={{height:"100%",width:`${pct}%`,background:"linear-gradient(90deg,#C9A84C,#E8C66A)",borderRadius:3,transition:"width .7s cubic-bezier(.16,1,.3,1)"}}/></div>
    <span style={{fontSize:11,color:"#6B6B8A",whiteSpace:"nowrap"}}>{xp%120}/120</span>
  </div>);
}

function TimerRing({sure,maxSure}){
  const pct=Math.max(0,sure/maxSure),sz=72,st=5,r=(sz-st)/2,circ=2*Math.PI*r,offset=circ*(1-pct);
  return(<div style={{position:"relative",width:sz,height:sz,flexShrink:0}}><svg width={sz} height={sz} style={{transform:"rotate(-90deg)"}}><circle cx={sz/2} cy={sz/2} r={r} fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.06)" strokeWidth={st}/><circle cx={sz/2} cy={sz/2} r={r} fill="none" stroke={sure<=10?"#EF4444":"#C9A84C"} strokeWidth={st} strokeLinecap="round" strokeDasharray={circ} strokeDashoffset={offset} style={{transition:"stroke-dashoffset .9s linear"}}/></svg><div style={{position:"absolute",inset:0,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}><span style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:700,color:sure<=10?"#EF4444":"#C9A84C",fontFamily:"Cinzel,serif"}}>{sure}</span></div></div>);
}
/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   KAVRAM EŞLEŞTİRME MODU (DÜZELTİLDİ & GERİ BUTONU EKLENDİ)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function EslestirmeEkrani({onBitis, onMenu}){
  const set = useMemo(() => ESLESTIRME_SETLERI[Math.floor(Math.random()*ESLESTIRME_SETLERI.length)], []);
  const [sure,setSure]=useState(50);
  const [timerAktif,setTimerAktif]=useState(true);
  const [seciliTerim,setSeciliTerim]=useState(null);
  const [eslesmis,setEslesmis]=useState({});
  const [hataModal,setHataModal]=useState(null);
  const [skor,setSkor]=useState(0);
  const timerRef=useRef(null);

  // Karşılıkların her saniye yer değiştirmemesi için useMemo ile sabitlendi
  const karistirKarsiliklist = useMemo(() => [...set.ciftler].sort(()=>Math.random()-.5).map(c=>c.karsilik), [set]);

  useEffect(()=>{
    if(!timerAktif||hataModal) return;
    timerRef.current=setInterval(()=>{
      setSure(s=>{
        if(s<=1){
          clearInterval(timerRef.current);
          onBitis({dogru:Object.keys(eslesmis).length,yanlis:0,xp:skor,toplam:set.ciftler.length,modLabel:"Eşleştirme"});
          return 0;
        }
        return s-1;
      });
    },1000);
    return()=>clearInterval(timerRef.current);
  },[timerAktif,hataModal,eslesmis,skor,set,onBitis]);

  const tiklaKarsilik=(karsilik)=>{
    if(!seciliTerim) return;
    const dogru=set.ciftler.find(c=>c.terim===seciliTerim)?.karsilik;
    if(karsilik===dogru){
      const yeni={...eslesmis,[seciliTerim]:karsilik};
      setEslesmis(yeni); setSkor(s=>s+20); setSeciliTerim(null);
      if(Object.keys(yeni).length===set.ciftler.length){
        clearInterval(timerRef.current);
        setTimeout(()=>onBitis({dogru:set.ciftler.length,yanlis:0,xp:skor+20,toplam:set.ciftler.length,modLabel:"Eşleştirme"}),500);
      }
    } else {
      setHataModal({terim:seciliTerim,aciklama:set.aciklamalar[seciliTerim]});
    }
  };

  return(<div style={{minHeight:"100vh",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",position:"relative",zIndex:1}} className="fade-in">
    <div style={{background:"rgba(10,10,20,.92)",backdropFilter:"blur(12px)",borderBottom:"1px solid rgba(34,211,238,.2)",padding:"14px 20px",display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center"}}>
      <button onClick={onMenu} style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.05)",border:"1px solid rgba(34,211,238,.3)",color:"#22D3EE",padding:"6px 12px",borderRadius:8,cursor:"pointer",fontSize:12,fontWeight:700}}>⬅ MENÜ</button>
      <div style={{textAlign:"center"}}><div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:600,color:"#22D3EE"}}>Kavram Eşleştirme</div></div>
      <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:sure<=10?"#EF4444":"#22D3EE",fontFamily:"Cinzel"}}>{sure}s</div>
    </div>
    <div style={{flex:1,padding:20,overflowY:"auto"}}>
      <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:10}}>
        <div style={{display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:8}}>
          {set.ciftler.map(c=>(
            <button key={c.terim} onClick={()=>setSeciliTerim(c.terim)} disabled={!!eslesmis[c.terim]}
              style={{padding:15,borderRadius:12,background:eslesmis[c.terim]?"rgba(16,185,129,.1)":seciliTerim===c.terim?"rgba(34,211,238,.2)":"rgba(255,255,255,.03)",border:`1.5px solid ${seciliTerim===c.terim?"#22D3EE":"rgba(255,255,255,.08)"}`,color:eslesmis[c.terim]?"#10B981":"#fff",cursor:"pointer",minHeight:60,fontSize:13,fontWeight:600}}>{c.terim}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:8}}>
          {karistirKarsiliklist.map(k=>(
            <button key={k} onClick={()=>tiklaKarsilik(k)} disabled={Object.values(eslesmis).includes(k)}
              style={{padding:15,borderRadius:12,background:Object.values(eslesmis).includes(k)?"rgba(16,185,129,.1)":"rgba(255,255,255,.03)",border:"1.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,.08)",color:Object.values(eslesmis).includes(k)?"#10B981":"#B0B0CC",cursor:"pointer",minHeight:60,fontSize:11}}>{k}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    {hataModal&&<div className="fade-in" style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,background:"rgba(4,4,14,.93)",zIndex:200,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",padding:16}}>
      <div className="pop-in" style={{background:"#0F0F1C",border:"1.5px solid #EF4444",borderRadius:22,padding:26,maxWidth:420,width:"100%"}}>
        <h3 style={{color:"#EF4444",marginBottom:10,fontFamily:"Cinzel"}}>Yanlış Eşleştirme!</h3>
        <p style={{color:"#C9A84C",fontSize:14,lineHeight:1.6,marginBottom:20}}>{hataModal.aciklama}</p>
        <button onClick={()=>{setHataModal(null);setSeciliTerim(null);}} style={{width:"100%",padding:14,background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#22D3EE,#0891B2)",border:"none",borderRadius:12,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",color:"#000"}}>ANLADIM, DEVAM ET</button>
      </div>
    </div>}
  </div>);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MODALLAR & ANALİZ (ORİJİNAL TASARIM)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function YanlisModal({soru,onDevam,surebitti}){
  const dogru=soru.secenekler.find(s=>s.harf===soru.dogru);
  return(<div className="fade-in" style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,background:"rgba(4,4,14,.93)",zIndex:200,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",padding:16}}><div className="pop-in" style={{background:"#0F0F1C",border:"1.5px solid #EF4444",borderRadius:22,padding:26,maxWidth:520,width:"100%"}}>
    <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:12,marginBottom:18}}><div style={{fontSize:22}}>{surebitti?"⏱️":"✗"}</div><div style={{fontSize:17,fontWeight:700,color:"#EF4444"}}>{surebitti?"Süre Doldu!":"Yanlış Cevap!"}</div></div>
    <div style={{background:"rgba(16,185,129,.09)",border:"1px solid #10B98133",borderRadius:12,padding:14,marginBottom:16}}><div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:700,color:"#10B981",marginBottom:6}}>DOĞRU CEVAP</div><div style={{fontSize:14}}><b style={{marginRight:8}}>{soru.dogru})</b>{dogru?.metin}</div></div>
    <div style={{background:"rgba(139,92,246,.08)",border:"1px solid #8B5CF644",borderRadius:12,padding:15,marginBottom:20}}><div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:700,color:"#8B5CF6",marginBottom:10}}>AÇIKLAMA</div><p style={{fontSize:13,lineHeight:1.7,color:"#A0A0C0"}}>{soru.aciklama}</p></div>
    <button onClick={onDevam} className="glow-btn" style={{width:"100%",padding:15,borderRadius:13,background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#8B5CF6,#6D28D9)",color:"#fff",fontWeight:700,border:"none",cursor:"pointer"}}>DEVAM ET →</button>
  </div></div>);
}

function DogruModal({xp,onDevam}){
  return(<div className="fade-in" style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,background:"rgba(4,4,14,.88)",zIndex:200,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}><div className="pop-in" style={{background:"#0F0F1C",border:"1.5px solid #10B981",borderRadius:22,padding:32,maxWidth:300,textAlign:"center"}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:50,marginBottom:10}}>✓</div><div style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:700,color:"#10B981",fontFamily:"Cinzel",marginBottom:20}}>DOĞRU!</div>
    <div style={{background:"rgba(201,168,76,.15)",padding:"7px 20px",borderRadius:20,color:"#C9A84C",fontWeight:700,marginBottom:25}}>+{xp} XP</div>
    <button onClick={onDevam} style={{width:"100%",padding:14,borderRadius:13,background:"#10B981",color:"#fff",fontWeight:700,border:"none",cursor:"pointer"}}>SIRADAKİ →</button>
  </div></div>);
}

function AnalizPaneli({istatistik,yanlislar,onKapat}){
  return(<div className="fade-in" style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,background:"rgba(4,4,14,.98)",zIndex:300,overflowY:"auto",padding:24}}><div style={{maxWidth:480,margin:"0 auto"}}>
    <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:20}}><h2 style={{fontFamily:"Cinzel",color:"#C9A84C"}}>Analiz Paneli</h2><button onClick={onKapat} style={{color:"#fff",background:"#EF4444",border:"none",padding:"8px 15px",borderRadius:8,cursor:"pointer"}}>✕ KAPAT</button></div>
    <div style={{background:"#0F0F1C",padding:20,borderRadius:18,border:"1px solid #ffffff11",marginBottom:20}}>
      <h3 style={{fontSize:14,color:"#6B6B8A",marginBottom:15}}>Konu Başarısı</h3>
      {KONU_ANALIZ.map(k=>{
        const kd=istatistik.konular[k.key]||{dogru:0,toplam:0};
        const pct=kd.toplam>0?Math.round((kd.dogru/kd.toplam)*100):0;
        return(<div key={k.key} style={{marginBottom:15}}><div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",fontSize:12,marginBottom:5}}><span>{k.label}</span><span>%{pct}</span></div>
          <div style={{height:6,background:"#ffffff08",borderRadius:3}}><div style={{height:"100%",width:`${pct}%`,background:k.renk,borderRadius:3,transition:"1s"}}/></div></div>);
      })}
    </div>
    <div style={{background:"#0F0F1C",padding:20,borderRadius:18,border:"1px solid #EF444433"}}><h3 style={{fontSize:14,color:"#EF4444",marginBottom:10}}>Tekrar Listesi ({yanlislar.length})</h3>
      {yanlislar.slice(-5).map((s,i)=><div key={i} style={{fontSize:11,color:"#A0A0C0",padding:"8px 0",borderBottom:"1px solid #ffffff05"}}>{s.soru.slice(0,70)}...</div>)}
    </div>
  </div></div>);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   SORU EKRANI (GERİ BUTONU EKLENDİ)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function SoruEkrani({mod,yanlisHavuz,onBitis,onYanlisEkle,onKonuGuncelle, onMenu}){
  const modInfo=MODLAR.find(m=>m.id===mod)||MODLAR[0];
  const [sorular,setSorular]=useState(null);
  const [idx,setIdx]=useState(0);
  const [sure,setSure]=useState(modInfo.sure);
  const [timerAktif,setTimerAktif]=useState(false);
  const [secilen,setSecilen]=useState(null);
  const [modal,setModal]=useState(null);
  const [skor,setSkor]=useState({dogru:0,yanlis:0,xp:0});
  const timerRef=useRef(null);

  useEffect(()=>{
    getModSorular(mod).then(s=>{
      const list = mod==="yanlis_tekrar" ? Object.values(yanlisHavuz) : s;
      setSorular(list); setTimerAktif(true);
    });
  },[mod, yanlisHavuz]);

  useEffect(()=>{
    if(!timerAktif||modal||!sorular?.[idx]) return;
    timerRef.current=setInterval(()=>{
      setSure(s=>{ if(s<=1){ clearInterval(timerRef.current); setModal("surebitti"); return 0; } return s-1; });
    },1000);
    return()=>clearInterval(timerRef.current);
  },[timerAktif,modal,idx,sorular]);

  const cevapla=(harf)=>{
    if(secilen||modal) return;
    clearInterval(timerRef.current); setSecilen(harf);
    const soru = sorular[idx];
    if(harf===soru.dogru){
      const kazanc = xpHesapla(sure,modInfo.sure,soru.zorluk);
      setSkor(p=>({...p,dogru:p.dogru+1,xp:p.xp+kazanc}));
      onKonuGuncelle(soru.konuKisa,true); setTimeout(()=>setModal("dogru"),400);
    } else {
      setSkor(p=>({...p,yanlis:p.yanlis+1}));
      onYanlisEkle(soru); onKonuGuncelle(soru.konuKisa,false); setTimeout(()=>setModal("yanlis"),400);
    }
  };

  const sonraki=()=>{ setModal(null); setSecilen(null); setSure(modInfo.sure); 
    if(idx+1>=sorular.length) onBitis({...skor, toplam:sorular.length, modLabel:modInfo.label});
    else { setIdx(idx+1); setTimerAktif(true); }
  };

  if(!sorular||sorular.length===0) return <div style={{height:"100vh",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",flexDirection:"column"}}>
    <p>Soru bulunamadı!</p><button onClick={onMenu} style={{marginTop:20,padding:10,background:"#C9A84C",border:"none",borderRadius:8}}>MENÜYE DÖN</button>
  </div>;

  return(<div style={{minHeight:"100vh",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
    <div style={{background:"rgba(10,10,20,.92)",backdropFilter:"blur(12px)",borderBottom:"1px solid #C9A84C33",padding:"14px 20px"}}>
      <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:12}}>
        <button onClick={onMenu} style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.05)",border:"1px solid #C9A84C55",color:"#C9A84C",padding:"6px 12px",borderRadius:8,cursor:"pointer",fontSize:12,fontWeight:700}}>⬅ MENÜ</button>
        <div style={{fontSize:12,color:"#6B6B8A"}}>{idx+1} / {sorular.length}</div>
      </div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:15}}><XPBar xp={skor.xp}/><TimerRing sure={sure} maxSure={modInfo.sure}/></div>
    </div>
    <div style={{flex:1,padding:"25px 20px"}} className="fade-up">
      <div style={{fontSize:11,color:modInfo.renk,marginBottom:10,fontWeight:700}}>{sorular[idx].konuKisa} · {sorular[idx].zorluk.toUpperCase()}</div>
      <div style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.03)",border:"1px solid #C9A84C33",padding:20,borderRadius:16,marginBottom:20,fontFamily:"Cinzel",lineHeight:1.6,fontSize:15}}>{sorular[idx].soru}</div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:10}}>{sorular[idx].secenekler.map(opt=>(
        <button key={opt.harf} onClick={()=>cevapla(opt.harf)} disabled={!!secilen}
          style={{display:"flex",padding:15,borderRadius:13,background:"#ffffff04",border:"1.5px solid #ffffff11",color:"#B0B0CC",textAlign:"left",cursor:"pointer",transition:".2s"}}>
          <b style={{color:"#C9A84C",marginRight:12}}>{opt.harf})</b>{opt.metin}</button>
      ))}</div>
    </div>
    {modal==="dogru"&&<DogruModal xp={xpHesapla(sure,modInfo.sure,sorular[idx].zorluk)} onDevam={sonraki}/>}
    {(modal==="yanlis"||modal==="surebitti")&&<YanlisModal soru={sorular[idx]} onDevam={sonraki} surebitti={modal==="surebitti"}/>}
  </div>);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   DASHBOARD & SONUÇ
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function Dashboard({onBasla,istatistik,yanlisHavuz,onAnalizAc}){
  const [secilen,setSecilen]=useState(null);
  const yanlisSayisi=Object.keys(yanlisHavuz).length;
  return(<div className="fade-in" style={{maxWidth:480,margin:"0 auto",padding:"30px 20px",position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
    <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:30}}><h1 style={{fontFamily:"Cinzel",fontSize:28,background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#C9A84C,#8B5CF6)",WebkitBackgroundClip:"text",WebkitTextFillColor:"transparent"}}>Tarih Akademisi</h1><p style={{fontSize:11,color:"#6B6B8A",letterSpacing:2,marginTop:5}}>KPSS LİSANS 2025</p></div>
    <div style={{background:"#0F0F1C",padding:20,borderRadius:20,border:"1px solid #C9A84C33",marginBottom:15}}>
      <XPBar xp={istatistik.xp}/><div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",marginTop:15,paddingTop:15,borderTop:"1px solid #ffffff05"}}>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center"}}><div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:"#10B981"}}>{istatistik.dogru}</div><div style={{fontSize:10,color:"#6B6B8A"}}>DOĞRU</div></div>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center"}}><div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:"#EF4444"}}>{istatistik.yanlis}</div><div style={{fontSize:10,color:"#6B6B8A"}}>YANLIŞ</div></div>
        <button onClick={onAnalizAc} style={{background:"#8B5CF615",border:"1px solid #8B5CF6",color:"#8B5CF6",borderRadius:8,padding:"5px 15px",fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer"}}>📊 ANALİZ</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    {yanlisSayisi>0&&<button onClick={()=>onBasla("yanlis_tekrar")} style={{width:"100%",padding:14,borderRadius:14,background:"#EF444411",border:"1.5px solid #EF4444",color:"#EF4444",fontWeight:700,marginBottom:15,cursor:"pointer"}}>🔁 YANLIŞLARINI TEKRARLA ({yanlisSayisi})</button>}
    <div style={{display:"grid",gap:8,maxHeight:350,overflowY:"auto",paddingRight:5}}>{MODLAR.map(m=>(
      <button key={m.id} onClick={()=>setSecilen(m.id)}
        style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:15,padding:14,borderRadius:16,background:secilen===m.id?`${m.renk}15`:"#0F0F1C",border:`1.5px solid ${secilen===m.id?m.renk:"#ffffff08"}`,color:"#fff",textAlign:"left",cursor:"pointer",transition:".2s"}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:22}}>{m.icon}</div><div style={{flex:1}}><div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:600}}>{m.label}</div><div style={{fontSize:10,color:"#6B6B8A"}}>{m.desc}</div></div>
      </button>
    ))}</div>
    <button onClick={()=>secilen&&onBasla(secilen)} disabled={!secilen} className={secilen?"glow-btn":""}
      style={{width:"100%",padding:18,marginTop:20,borderRadius:15,background:secilen?"linear-gradient(135deg,#C9A84C,#E8C66A)":"#222",color:"#07070F",fontWeight:800,fontSize:15,fontFamily:"Cinzel",border:"none",cursor:secilen?"pointer":"default"}}>SINAVI BAŞLAT →</button>
  </div>);
}

function SonucEkrani({sonuc,onMenu}){
  return(<div className="fade-up" style={{height:"100vh",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",padding:25,position:"relative",zIndex:1,textAlign:"center"}}>
    <h2 style={{fontFamily:"Cinzel",color:"#C9A84C",fontSize:30,marginBottom:10}}>Sınav Bitti!</h2><p style={{color:"#6B6B8A",fontSize:13}}>{sonuc.modLabel} Modu Tamamlandı</p>
    <div style={{margin:"30px 0"}}><div style={{fontSize:45,fontWeight:900,color:"#8B5CF6",textShadow:"0 0 20px #8B5CF644"}}>+{sonuc.xp} XP</div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:15,marginTop:20}}>
        <div style={{background:"#10B98111",padding:"15px 25px",borderRadius:15,border:"1.5px solid #10B981",color:"#10B981"}}><b>{sonuc.dogru}</b> Doğru</div>
        <div style={{background:"#EF444411",padding:"15px 25px",borderRadius:15,border:"1.5px solid #EF4444",color:"#EF4444"}}><b>{sonuc.yanlis}</b> Yanlış</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <button onClick={onMenu} style={{padding:"16px 45px",borderRadius:15,background:"#C9A84C",color:"#07070F",fontWeight:800,border:"none",cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"Cinzel"}}>ANA MENÜYE DÖN</button>
  </div>);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   ROOT APP (DÜZENLENDİ)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
export default function App(){
  const [ekran,setEkran]=useState("menu");
  const [aktifMod,setAktifMod]=useState(null);
  const [sonuc,setSonuc]=useState(null);
  const [analizAcik,setAnalizAcik]=useState(false);
  const [istatistik,setIstatistik]=useStorage("kpss_istat_v3",{dogru:0,yanlis:0,xp:0,toplam:0,konular:{}});
  const [yanlisHavuz,setYanlisHavuz]=useStorage("kpss_yanlis_v3",{});

  const yanlisEkle=useCallback((soru)=>{ setYanlisHavuz(prev=>prev[soru.id]?prev:{...prev,[soru.id]:soru}); },[setYanlisHavuz]);
  const konuGuncelle=useCallback((konuKisa,dogru)=>{
    setIstatistik(prev=>{
      const k=prev.konular[konuKisa]||{dogru:0,toplam:0};
      return{...prev,konular:{...prev.konular,[konuKisa]:{dogru:k.dogru+(dogru?1:0),toplam:k.toplam+1}}};
    });
  },[setIstatistik]);

  const basla=(mod)=>{setAktifMod(mod);setEkran("oyun");};
  const bitis=(s)=>{
    setIstatistik(prev=>({...prev,dogru:prev.dogru+s.dogru,yanlis:prev.yanlis+s.yanlis,xp:prev.xp+s.xp,toplam:prev.toplam+s.toplam}));
    setSonuc(s);setEkran("sonuc");
  };

  return(<>
    <style>{CSS}</style>
    <StarCanvas/>
    <div style={{position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
      {ekran==="menu"&&<Dashboard onBasla={basla} istatistik={istatistik} yanlisHavuz={yanlisHavuz} onAnalizAc={()=>setAnalizAcik(true)}/>}
      {ekran==="oyun"&&aktifMod==="eslestirme"&&<EslestirmeEkrani onBitis={bitis} onMenu={()=>setEkran("menu")}/>}
      {ekran==="oyun"&&aktifMod&&aktifMod!=="eslestirme"&&
        <SoruEkrani mod={aktifMod} yanlisHavuz={yanlisHavuz} onBitis={bitis} onYanlisEkle={yanlisEkle} onKonuGuncelle={konuGuncelle} onMenu={()=>setEkran("menu")}/>}
      {ekran==="sonuc"&&sonuc&&<SonucEkrani sonuc={sonuc} onMenu={()=>setEkran("menu")}/>}
      {analizAcik&&<AnalizPaneli istatistik={istatistik} yanlislar={Object.values(yanlisHavuz)} onKapat={()=>setAnalizAcik(false)}/>}
    </div>
  </>);
}
